\hypertarget{classcryptonote_1_1simple__wallet}{}\doxysection{cryptonote\+::simple\+\_\+wallet Class Reference}

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Manages wallet operations. This is the most abstracted wallet class.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void cryptonote\+::simple\+\_\+wallet\+::commit\+\_\+or\+\_\+save (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classtools_1_1wallet2_abb47f9fb6f6f57be4f2a7be685514d0d}{tools\+::wallet2\+::pending\+\_\+tx}} $>$ \&}]{ptx\+\_\+vector,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}}}]{do\+\_\+not\+\_\+relay,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}}}]{blink }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Submits or saves the transaction. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ptx\+\_\+vector} & Pending tx(es) created by transfer/sweep\+\_\+all \\
\hline
{\em do\+\_\+not\+\_\+relay} & if true, save the raw tx hex blob to a file instead of calling m\+\_\+wallet-\/$>$commit\+\_\+tx(ptx). \\
\hline
{\em blink} & true if this should be submitted as a blink tx \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
